	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: 3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js');
	$tmp = pathinfo('3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}

	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): 3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js');

} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of 3p/bcrypt.js/bcrypt.js');
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/oidplus_base.js');
	writefile_7();
	if (!is_file('includes/oidplus_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') != '4c1e0452ba07d668cd0d0f3d9e9e10c7b4ebd0b2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/oidplus_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/oidplus_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '4c1e0452ba07d668cd0d0f3d9e9e10c7b4ebd0b2') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== 'cb0ddb15fc20bbe1c13eb0516aa040d02115218e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/oidplus_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/oidplus_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/oidplus_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_7();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/oidplus_base.js') !== '4c1e0452ba07d668cd0d0f3d9e9e10c7b4ebd0b2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/oidplus_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	writefile_21();
	if (!is_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') != '68926cdca6b92b073599a109ceba1bf8d10eb9ed') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '68926cdca6b92b073599a109ceba1bf8d10eb9ed') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '17587d786632be361c569dbbf1633205afcfadf2') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_21();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '68926cdca6b92b073599a109ceba1bf8d10eb9ed') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/language/dede/messages.xml');
		}
	}
}

		if (@sha1_file('plugins/raPages/092_invite/OIDplusPageRaInvite.js') !== '85bbdeb40da28aebe64e3e1ae61da42db8bacae1') {

if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	writefile_38();
	if (!is_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') != 'da0a02cef606baf10e307bde3d785efcc2983349') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/includes/setup_base.js', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/includes/setup_base.js');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== 'da0a02cef606baf10e307bde3d785efcc2983349') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== 'f8b65da419a8ed37402ffb729080850c74f40a73') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/includes/setup_base.js');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/includes/setup_base.js')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/includes/setup_base.js', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_38();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/includes/setup_base.js') !== 'da0a02cef606baf10e307bde3d785efcc2983349') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/includes/setup_base.js');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/index.php');
	writefile_39();
	if (!is_file('setup/index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/index.php') != '9d2aa87685b596d16d637266d9125c552fa9de66') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '9d2aa87685b596d16d637266d9125c552fa9de66') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '265561329ba7fe446f8fd6b6753459c2fc115b33') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_39();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/index.php') !== '9d2aa87685b596d16d637266d9125c552fa9de66') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/index.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: setup/setup.min.js.php');
	writefile_40();
	if (!is_file('setup/setup.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') != '47ef1441280bdceaf32d6fc7d11f992dc4480088') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('setup/setup.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of setup/setup.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '47ef1441280bdceaf32d6fc7d11f992dc4480088') {
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '91f01a524ed1ac99b6835b86d899ea1d4e783261') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('setup/setup.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('setup/setup.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('setup/setup.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_40();
		if (@sha1_file('setup/setup.min.js.php') !== '47ef1441280bdceaf32d6fc7d11f992dc4480088') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): setup/setup.min.js.php');
		}
	}
}

if (is_file('setup/bcrypt_worker.js')) {
	warn('File could not be deleted: setup/bcrypt_worker.js');
}
